Source Code

This source code is very close to the Apollo Guidance Computer software for the Apollo 13 Lunar module. This revision of the Luminary 131 program is from December of 1969, whereas there was a later revision in January of 1970, and still another revision in February, which is the code that flew on the mission. As far as this transcription is concerned, it was originally from a copy made in 1991 of a printout from the collection of AGC developer Don Eyles for collector David Craig. It was subsequently scanned by Gary Neff, reprocessed for online presentation at the now-discontinued History of Recent Science and Technology (HRST) website of MIT's Dibner Institute (the full-quality scans being discarded in the process), and finally transcribed by Ron Burkey for the Virtual AGC Project. Although a high-quality replacement scan for a completely illegible page was later provided by Gary Neff, the reduced legibility of the reprocessed HRST posting nevertheless caused many errors to be introduced into the transcription. Accordingly, a second scan of the same physical printout was made in 2017 for the Virtual AGC Project's collection at the Internet Archive, and used to correct the transcription errors. All of the scanned materials mentioned, as well as other Luminary 131 related material, are available online. Don Eyles apprently made additional hand-written notes in printout between 1991 and 2017, so the two scans are not identical in that respect. The page-headings in the printout read, in part:
	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 131 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-091
	17:53 DEC. 19, 1969
Note that the date is the date the printout was made, not the date on which the program revision was released, although these happen to be very close together.

016369,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME_BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
016370,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Luminary 1C, revision 131.
016371,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the Lunar Module's (LM)
016372,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13.
016373,000007:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
016374,000008:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
016375,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the 
016376,000010:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
016377,000011:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 392-475
016378,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
016379,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo

016404,000038:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016405,000039:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016406,000040:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016407,000041:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016408,000042: 
016409,000043:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016410,000044: 
016411,000045:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016412,000046:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016413,000047:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016414,000048:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016415,000049: 
016416,000050:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016417,000051:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016418,000052:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016419,000053:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016420,000054:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016421,000055: 
016422,000056:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016423,000057:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016424,000058:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016425,000059:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016426,000060: 
016427,000061:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016428,000062:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016429,000063: 
016430,000064:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016431,000065: 
016432,000066:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016433,000067:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016434,000068:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016435,000069:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016436,000070:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016437,000071: 
016438,000072:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016439,000073:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016440,000074:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016441,000075:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016442,000076: 
016443,000077:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016444,000078:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016445,000079:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016446,000080:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016447,000081:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016448,000082: 
016449,000083:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016450,000084: 
016451,000085:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016452,000086:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016453,000087:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 393 

016455,000089:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016456,000090:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016457,000091:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016458,000092:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016459,000093:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016460,000094:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016461,000095:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016462,000096:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016463,000097:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016464,000098:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016465,000099: 
016466,000100:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016467,000101:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016468,000102:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016469,000103: 
016470,000104:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016471,000105: 
016472,000106:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016473,000107:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016474,000108:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016475,000109: 
016476,000110:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016477,000111:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016478,000112:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016479,000113:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016480,000114:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016481,000115:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016482,000116:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016483,000117: 
016484,000118:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016485,000119:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016486,000120: 
016487,000121:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016488,000122: 
016489,000123:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016490,000124:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016491,000125:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016492,000126:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016493,000127: 
016494,000128:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016495,000129: 
016496,000130:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016497,000131:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016498,000132:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016499,000133:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016500,000134: 
016501,000135:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 394 

016503,000137:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016504,000138: 
016505,000139:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016506,000140: 
016507,000141:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016508,000142:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016509,000143: 
016510,000144:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016511,000145:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016512,000146:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016513,000147:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016514,000148: 
016515,000149:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016516,000150:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016517,000151: 
016518,000152:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016519,000153:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016520,000154:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016521,000155:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016522,000156: 
016523,000157:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016524,000158:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016525,000159: 
016526,000160:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016527,000161:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
016528,000162: 
016529,000163:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016530,000164: 
016531,000165:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016532,000166:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016533,000167:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016534,000168:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016535,000169: 
016536,000170:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016537,000171:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016538,000172: 
016539,000173:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016540,000174:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016541,000175: 
016542,000176:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016543,000177:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016544,000178:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016545,000179: 
016546,000180:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
016547,000181: 
016548,000182:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
016549,000183:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO

Page 395 

016551,000185:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
016552,000186:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
016553,000187: 
016554,000188:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
016555,000189: 
016556,000190: 
016557,000191:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016558,000192: 
016559,000193:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
016560,000194:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
016561,000195:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
016562,000196:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
016563,000197:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
016564,000198:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
016565,000199:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
016566,000200:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016567,000201:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016568,000202:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016569,000203:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
016570,000204:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
016571,000205:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
016572,000206:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
016573,000207:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
016574,000208:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
016575,000209:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
016576,000210:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
016577,000211:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
016578,000212:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
016579,000213:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
016580,000214:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
016581,000215:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE +1
016582,000216:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016583,000217:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
016584,000218:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
016585,000219:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
016586,000220:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
016587,000221:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
016588,000222:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
016589,000223:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
016590,000224:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
016591,000225:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
016592,000226:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
016593,000227:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
016594,000228:

016596,000230:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

016650,000284:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
016651,000285:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
016652,000286:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
016653,000287:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
016654,000288:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
016655,000289:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
016656,000290:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
016657,000291:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
016658,000292:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016659,000293:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016660,000294:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016661,000295:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
016662,000296:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016663,000297:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
016664,000298:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016665,000299:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
016666,000300:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
016667,000301: 
016668,000302:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016669,000303: 
016670,000304:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
016671,000305: 
016672,000306:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
016673,000307:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
016674,000308:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
016675,000309:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
016676,000310:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
016677,000311: 
016678,000312:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
016679,000313: 
016680,000314:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016681,000315: 
016682,000316:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
016683,000317:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
016684,000318:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
016685,000319: 
016686,000320:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016687,000321: 
016688,000322:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016689,000323: 
016690,000324:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016691,000325:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
016692,000326:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
016693,000327: 
016694,000328:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
016695,000329:

Page 398 

016697,000331:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
016698,000332:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
016699,000333:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
016700,000334:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
016701,000335:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
016702,000336:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
016703,000337:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
016704,000338:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
016705,000339:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
016706,000340:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
016707,000341:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
016708,000342:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
016709,000343: 
016710,000344:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016711,000345:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016712,000346:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016713,000347:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016714,000348:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016715,000349:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016716,000350: 
016717,000351:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016718,000352:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
016719,000353:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
016720,000354:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
016721,000355:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
016722,000356:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
016723,000357: 
016724,000358:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016725,000359: 
016726,000360:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016727,000361:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
016728,000362:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
016729,000363:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
016730,000364:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
016731,000365:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
016732,000366:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
016733,000367:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
016734,000368:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
016735,000369:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
016736,000370:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
016737,000371: 
016738,000372:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016739,000373: 
016740,000374:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016741,000375:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
016742,000376:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016743,000377:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016744,000378:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016745,000379:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 399 

016747,000381:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016748,000382:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016749,000383:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016750,000384:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016751,000385:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016752,000386:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016753,000387:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016754,000388:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
016755,000389: 
016756,000390:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016757,000391: 
016758,000392:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
016759,000393:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
016760,000394:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
016761,000395:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
016762,000396:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
016763,000397:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
016764,000398:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
016765,000399:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
016766,000400:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
016767,000401:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
016768,000402:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
016769,000403: 
016770,000404:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016771,000405: 
016772,000406:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016773,000407:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016774,000408:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
016775,000409:

017173,000807:                                                                                                  #  ENTER PASS 0 IS THE EXECUTE FUNCTION.  HIGHER ORDER ENTERS ARE TO LOAD
017174,000808:                                                                                                  #  DATA.  THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
017175,000809:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.
017176,000810: 
017177,000811:                                                                                                  #  MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED (MCTBS) NOUNS DESIRE AN ECADR TO BE LOADED
017178,000812:                                                                                                  #  WHEN USED WITH LOAD VERBS, MONITOR VERBS, OR DISPLAY VERBS (EXCEPT
017179,000813:                                                                                                  #  VERB = FIXED MEMORY DISPLAY, WHICH REQUIRES AN FCADR).

Page 415 

017466,001100:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017467,001101: 
017468,001102:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017469,001103:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
017470,001104:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017471,001105:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017472,001106:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017473,001107: 
017474,001108:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017475,001109:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017476,001110: 
017477,001111:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017478,001112: 
017479,001113:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017480,001114:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017481,001115:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017482,001116: 
017483,001117:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017484,001118:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017485,001119:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017486,001120:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017487,001121:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017488,001122:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017489,001123: 
017490,001124:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017491,001125:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017492,001126:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017493,001127:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017494,001128:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017495,001129: 
017496,001130:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017497,001131:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017498,001132: 
017499,001133:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017500,001134: 
017501,001135:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017502,001136:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017503,001137:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017504,001138:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017505,001139:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017506,001140: 
017507,001141:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017508,001142:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017509,001143:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017510,001144: 
017511,001145:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017512,001146:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017513,001147: 
017514,001148:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017515,001149:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
017516,001150:

Page 416 

017518,001152:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017519,001153: 
017520,001154: 41,2355           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
017521,001155: 41,2356           02426                           TC       COMPTEST

018068,001702:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
018069,001703:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
018070,001704:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
018071,001705:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.

018692,002326: 42,3605           04145                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #  VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
018693,002327: 42,3606                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
018694,002328:

Page 441 

018696,002330:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018697,002331:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018698,002332:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018699,002333:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018700,002334:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018701,002335: 
018702,002336:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018703,002337:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018704,002338:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
018705,002339:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
018706,002340:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018707,002341:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018708,002342:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018709,002343: 
018710,002344:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018711,002345:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018712,002346:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018713,002347: 
018714,002348:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018715,002349:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018716,002350: 
018717,002351:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018718,002352:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018719,002353: 
018720,002354:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018846,002480:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018847,002481:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
018848,002482:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018849,002483:                                                                                                  #  
018850,002484:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018851,002485: 
018852,002486:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018853,002487:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018854,002488:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018855,002489: 
018856,002490:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018857,002491:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018858,002492:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018859,002493: 
018860,002494: 41,3400           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018861,002495: 41,3401           54776                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018862,002496: 41,3402           31046                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018863,002497: 41,3403           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018864,002498: 41,3404           31016                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018865,002499: 41,3405           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018866,002500: 41,3406           03410                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018867,002501: 41,3407           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

019266,002900:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
019267,002901:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE.  SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,

019274,002908: 
019275,002909:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
019276,002910:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.

Page 454 

019278,002912: 
019279,002913:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
019280,002914: 
019281,002915:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
019282,002916: 
019283,002917:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
019284,002918:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
019285,002919:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
019286,002920:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
019287,002921: 
019288,002922:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
019289,002923:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
019290,002924:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
019291,002925: 
019292,002926:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
019293,002927:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
019294,002928:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
019295,002929:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
019296,002930:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
019297,002931:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019298,002932:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019299,002933:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019300,002934:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019301,002935:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019302,002936:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019303,002937: 
019304,002938: 40,3524           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019305,002939: 40,3525           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019306,002940: 40,3526           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019307,002941: 40,3527           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019308,002942: 40,3530           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019309,002943: 40,3531           71020                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019310,002944: 40,3532           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019311,002945: 40,3533           03542                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019312,002946: 40,3534           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019313,002947: 40,3535           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019314,002948: 40,3536           03540                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019315,002949: 40,3537           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019316,002950: 40,3540           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019317,002951: 40,3541           21051                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019318,002952: 40,3542           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019319,002953: 40,3543           55011                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019320,002954: 40,3544           11041                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019321,002955: 40,3545           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019322,002956: 40,3546           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019323,002957: 40,3547           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019324,002958: 
019325,002959: 40,3550                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019326,002960:

Page 455 

019328,002962:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
019329,002963:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019330,002964:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019331,002965:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019332,002966:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019333,002967: 
019334,002968:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019335,002969:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
019336,002970:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019337,002971: 
019338,002972:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019339,002973:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019340,002974: 
019341,002975:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019342,002976:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019343,002977:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019344,002978:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019345,002979:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019346,002980: 
019347,002981:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019348,002982:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019349,002983:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019350,002984:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019351,002985: 
019352,002986:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019353,002987:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019354,002988:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019355,002989:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019356,002990:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019357,002991:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019358,002992:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019359,002993: 
019360,002994:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019361,002995:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019362,002996: 
019363,002997:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019364,002998:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019365,002999: 
019366,003000:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019367,003001:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019368,003002: 
019369,003003:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019370,003004:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019371,003005:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019372,003006:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019373,003007:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019374,003008:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019375,003009:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019376,003010: 
019377,003011:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 456 

019379,003013:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019380,003014:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019381,003015:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019382,003016:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019383,003017:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
019384,003018:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019385,003019:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019386,003020:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019387,003021:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019388,003022: 
019389,003023:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019390,003024:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019391,003025: 
019392,003026:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
019393,003027: 
019394,003028:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN
