019423,003057:    4203           05165                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
019424,003058:

019499,003133:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
019500,003134: 
019501,003135:    4204                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
019502,003136:    4204                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019503,003137:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019504,003138:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019505,003139:    4205           55020                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019506,003140:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019507,003141:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019508,003142: 
019509,003143:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
019510,003144:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019511,003145:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019512,003146:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019513,003147:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
019514,003148: 
019515,003149:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019516,003150:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019517,003151:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019518,003152:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019519,003153:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019520,003154:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019521,003155:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019522,003156:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019523,003157:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019524,003158:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019525,003159: 
019526,003160:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 459 

019528,003162:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019529,003163:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019530,003164:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019531,003165:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019532,003166:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
019533,003167: 
019534,003168:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019535,003169:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019536,003170:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019537,003171:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019538,003172:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019539,003173:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019540,003174:    4215           55041                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019541,003175:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019542,003176: 
019543,003177:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019544,003178: 
019545,003179:    4220           11041        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019546,003180:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

019586,003220: 
019587,003221:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
019588,003222:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
019589,003223:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
019590,003224:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
019591,003225:

019871,003505:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019872,003506: 
019873,003507:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019874,003508:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019875,003509:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019876,003510:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019877,003511: 
019878,003512:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019879,003513:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
019880,003514:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
019881,003515:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019882,003516:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019883,003517:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019884,003518:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019885,003519: 
019886,003520:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019887,003521:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019888,003522:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019889,003523:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019890,003524:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019891,003525: 
019892,003526:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019893,003527:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019894,003528:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019895,003529:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019896,003530:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019897,003531: 
019898,003532:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019899,003533:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019900,003534:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019901,003535: 
019902,003536: 
019903,003537:                                                                                                  #  .
019904,003538: 
019905,003539: 
019906,003540:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019907,003541:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019908,003542:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019909,003543:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019910,003544: 
019911,003545:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019912,003546:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019913,003547:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019914,003548: 
019915,003549:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019916,003550:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
019917,003551:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 468 

019919,003553:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019920,003554: 
019921,003555:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019922,003556:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019923,003557:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019924,003558:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019925,003559:    4443           10633                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019926,003560:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019927,003561: 
019928,003562:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019929,003563:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019930,003564: 
019931,003565: 04,2633                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019932,003566: 04,2633                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019933,003567: 04,2633           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019934,003568: 04,2634           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.

019940,003574: 
019941,003575:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019942,003576:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019943,003577:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019944,003578:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019945,003579:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019946,003580: 
019947,003581:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019948,003582:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

019954,003588:    4452           10000                           CCS      A

019956,003590:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019957,003591:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019958,003592:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019959,003593:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
